---
title: "SSD科普十五：Vth Tracking，为什么昨天能读对的数据，今天可能会读错？"
date: "2026-05-27 23:13:00"
tags: [SSD, 公众号]

<h1 style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 2rem 0px 0.5rem;padding: 0px;font-weight: 700;color: rgb(248, 95, 72);line-height: 1.35;font-size: 24px;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;font-family: Menlo, Monaco, &quot;Source Code Pro&quot;, Consolas, Inconsolata, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;DejaVu Sans Mono&quot;, &quot;Courier New&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, 微软雅黑, monospace !important;" data-pm-slice="0 0 []"><span leaf="">一、上一篇我们讲 Read Retry，这一篇要讲它背后的“追踪能力”</span></h1><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">前面我们讲过，NAND 读取数据，本质上不是像硬盘那样把一个稳定的 0 或 1 直接拿出来。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">NAND 读取更像是在问一个问题：</span></p><blockquote style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 1em 0px 1.2em;padding: 15px 15px 15px 1rem;color: rgb(129, 145, 152);font-weight: 400;border-left: 6px solid rgb(96, 125, initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 14px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);"><span leaf="">这个 cell 的阈值电压 Vth，到底落在哪个区间？</span></p></blockquote><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, initial;"><span leaf="">对于 TLC 来说，一个 cell 有 8 种状态。 对于 QLC 来说，一个 cell 有 16 种状态。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">所以 SSD 读取 NAND 的时候，不是简单判断“有电 / 没电”，而是要用一组 read level，把这些状态分开。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">它们会移动，会变宽，会互相靠近。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">于是原来好用的 read level，慢慢就不准了。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">这时候，就需要&nbsp;</span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;font-weight: bold;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);margin-top: 0px;"><span leaf="">Vth Tracking</span></strong><span leaf="">。</span></p><hr style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 1.5rem 0px;padding: 0px;border-width: 1px medium normal;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">二、什么是 Vth？</span></h2><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">Vth，全称是 threshold voltage，阈值电压。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">通俗说，就是：</span></p><blockquote style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 1em 0px 1.2em;padding: 15px 15px 15px 1rem;color: rgb(129, 145, 152);font-weight: 400;border-left: 6px solid rgb(96, 125, 139);font-size: 14px;line-height: 22px;background: rgb(242, 247, 251);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;white-space: normal;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 14px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);"><span leaf="">让一个 cell 从“不导通”变成“导通”所需要的控制栅电压。</span></p></blockquote><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">NAND 里面存数据，不是直接存 0 和 1，而是通过浮栅或者电荷捕获层里的电子数量，改变 cell 的阈值电压。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">电子越多，Vth 越高。 电子越少，Vth 越低。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">所以 NAND 里的数据，本质上是通过不同的 Vth 区间来表示的。</span></p><section style="text-align: center;" nodeleaf=""><img data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/95znLLjaNf8XjknFOJLMncdY1iaK6t9vJSDIiaKZicOicxWgrW9dKAzkmzrxYEZ2XhfFEZCWrmCglwcJlXJwrOCh747RovZfPUXicdp5uYwcnt3E/640?wx_fmt=png&amp;from=appmsg" initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">状态越多，每个状态之间的间隔就越小。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 15px;font-style: YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">这就是 Read Retry。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">但如果每次都靠 Read Retry，代价很高。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">因为每多 retry 一次，就多一次 NAND read。 读延迟会上升，性能会抖动，功耗也会增加。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">所以更好的办法不是每次都临时猜，而是：</span></p><blockquote style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 1em 0px 1.2em;padding: 15px 15px 15px 1rem;color: rgb(129, 145, 152);font-weight: 400;border-left: 6px solid rgb(96, 125, 139);font-size: 14px;line-height: 22px;background: rgb(242, 247, 251);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;white-space: normal;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 14px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);"><span leaf="">既然这块 NAND 的最佳 read level 已经偏了，那我能不能把这个偏移趋势记下来？</span></p></blockquote><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">这就是 Vth Tracking 的意义。</span></p><hr style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 1.5rem 0px;padding: 0px;border-width: 1px medium medium;border-style: dashed none none;border-color: rgb(165, 165, 165) currentcolor currentcolor;border-image: initial;height: 1px;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-size: 15px;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: 0px;white-space: normal;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 2rem 0px 0.5rem;padding: 0px;font-family: Menlo, Monaco, &quot;Source Code Pro&quot;, Consolas, Inconsolata, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;DejaVu Sans Mono&quot;, &quot;Courier New&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, 微软雅黑, monospace !important;font-weight: 700;color: rgb(248, 95, 72);line-height: 1.35;font-size: 24px;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">六、Vth Tracking 到底在 tracking 什么？</span></h2><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">Vth Tracking 不是直接去测每一个 cell 的真实 Vth。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">这在 SSD 运行时不现实。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 1rem;color: rgb(129, 145, 152);font-weight: 400;border-left: 6px solid rgb(96, 125, 139);font-size: 14px;line-height: 22px;background: rgb(242, 247, 251);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;white-space: normal;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 14px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);"><span leaf="">某个 block、某个 wordline、某类页面，在当前老化程度和环境条件下，更适合用哪一组 read level。</span></p></blockquote><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">也就是说，它追踪的是“最佳读取位置”的变化。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, 不会凭空知道。它通常要靠读取结果反推。最直接的线索是 ECC。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">一次 Read Retry 成功以后，SSD 不一定只是把数据返回给主机就结束。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">它让 SSD 从“每次都临时抢救”，变成“根据历史经验提前校准”。</span></p><hr style="box-sizing: &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;DejaVu Sans Mono&quot;, &quot;Courier New&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, 微软雅黑, monospace !important;font-weight: 700;color: rgb(248, initial;"><span leaf="">十、Vth Tracking 不是为了炫技，而是为了降低尾延迟</span></h2><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: initial;"><span leaf="">从用户角度看，Vth Tracking 最直接的价值不是“读得更科学”，而是：</span></p><blockquote style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 1em 0px 1.2em;padding: 15px 15px 15px 1rem;color: rgb(129, 145, 152);font-weight: 400;border-left: 6px solid rgb(96, 125, 139);font-size: 14px;line-height: 22px;background: rgb(242, 247, 251);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 14px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);"><span leaf="">减少 Read Retry 次数，降低读延迟抖动。</span></p></blockquote><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">普通读延迟可能很低。但一旦触发多次 Read Retry，延迟可能明显上升。这会形成所谓的 long tail latency，也就是尾延迟。平均延迟看起来还行，但偶尔某些读请求特别慢。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">对普通家用电脑来说，可能表现为偶发卡顿。 对企业级 SSD 来说，这就是很严重的问题。 因为数据库、存储系统、虚拟化环境都很怕尾延迟。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: style="box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 14px !important;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);margin-top: 0px;display: block;word-break: inherit !important;line-height: 22px;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 0px 0px 0px -20px;padding: 0px;font-style: normal;font-weight: 400;font-family: inherit !important;display: flex;overflow: initial;line-height: 12px;overflow-wrap: normal;border: 0px;font-size: 10px;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 13px !important;color: rgb(204, 204, 204);margin-top: 0px;line-height: 20px;white-space: inherit !important;font-family: consolas, menlo, courier, &quot;monospace&quot;, &quot;Microsoft Yahei&quot; !important;"><span leaf="">提高读稳定性</span></span></code></span></span></li></ol></pre><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">它不一定让每一次读取都更快，但它能减少那些特别慢的读取。</span></p><hr style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 1.5rem 0px;padding: 0px;border-width: 1px medium medium;border-style: dashed none none;border-color: rgb(165, 165, 165) currentcolor currentcolor;border-image: initial;height: 1px;font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;white-space: normal;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><h2 style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 2rem 0px 0.5rem;padding: 0px;font-family: Menlo, Monaco, &quot;Source Code Pro&quot;, Consolas, Inconsolata, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;DejaVu Sans Mono&quot;, &quot;Courier New&quot;, &quot;Droid Sans Mono&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, 微软雅黑, monospace !important;font-weight: 700;color: rgb(248, 95, 72);line-height: 1.35;font-size: 24px;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;white-space: normal;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">十一、Vth Tracking 也能保护 ECC 余量</span></h2><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">ECC 不是无限强的。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">如果一个 page 有 200 个 bit 错误，而 ECC 最多只能纠 220 个，那这次虽然成功了，但已经很危险。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">这就像考试刚好压线及格。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">你不能因为这次过了，就认为没问题。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">因为下次温度变了、放置时间更长了、read disturb 更多了，错误 bit 可能就超过 ECC 能力。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">Vth Tracking 的意义之一，就是尽量把读取点调到更合理的位置，让原始 bit error pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">一个比较形象的比喻是相机对焦。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">NAND 的 Vth 分布就像被拍摄的物体。 read level 就像相机的焦点。 ECC 就像后期修图。 Read Retry 就像发现照片糊了以后重新对焦再拍一张。 Vth Tracking 则是自动对焦系统。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: 300;letter-spacing: normal;orphans: 2;text-align: start;text-indent: 0px;text-transform: none;widows: 2;word-spacing: 0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px;text-decoration-thickness: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">刚开始，对焦位置是准的。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: normal;font-variant-ligatures: normal;font-variant-caps: normal;font-weight: initial;text-decoration-style: initial;text-decoration-color: initial;"><span leaf="">但随着物体移动、光线变化、镜头抖动，原来的焦点就不准了。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, &quot;PingFang SC&quot;, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei UI&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif;font-style: style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, -apple-system-font, 解决的是“下一次怎么不要再从头试错”。</span></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 15px 0px;padding: 0px;font-size: 15px;white-space: pre-line;line-height: 30px;color: rgb(74, 74, 74);font-family: mp-quote, 存储最有意思的地方：</span></p><blockquote style="box-sizing: border-box;margin: 1em 0px 1.2em;padding: 15px 15px 15px 1rem;color: rgb(129, 145, 152);font-weight: 400;border-left: 6px solid rgb(96, 125,
